<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переезжать.html>переезжа́ть</a> (10420)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-езжа́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jezžátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go (by vehicle)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переезжать.html>переезжа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perejezžátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переехать.html>перее́хать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to move <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to change residence</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:следующий.html>сле́дующей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неделя.html>неде́ле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переезжать.html>переезжа́ем</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:квартира.html>кварти́ру</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Na slédujuščej nedéle my <b>perejezžájem</b> na nóvuju kvartíru</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Next week we're moving to a new flat (apartment).</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cross, to run over, to drive over
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:опять.html>опя́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переехать.html>перее́хал</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шланг.html>шланг</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:теперь.html>тепе́рь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:протекать.html>протека́ет</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ty opjátʹ <b>perejéxal</b> šlang, on tepérʹ protekájet</i> ― <span class="e-translation">You've ran over the hose again, it's now leaking.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переехать.html>перее́хать</a> (4650)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>е́хать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jéxatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переехать.html>перее́хать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perejéxatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переезжать.html>переезжа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to move <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to change residence</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:следующий.html>сле́дующей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неделя.html>неде́ле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переезжать.html>переезжа́ем</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:квартира.html>кварти́ру</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Na slédujuščej nedéle my <b>perejezžájem</b> na nóvuju kvartíru</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Next week we're moving to a new flat (apartment).</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cross, to run over, to drive over
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:опять.html>опя́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переехать.html>перее́хал</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шланг.html>шланг</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:теперь.html>тепе́рь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:протекать.html>протека́ет</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ty opjátʹ <b>perejéxal</b> šlang, on tepérʹ protekájet</i> ― <span class="e-translation">You've run over the hose again, it's now leaking.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>пе<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ре.html>ре</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>е́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>хать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,   <a href = vnd.unilang:изолированный.html>изоли́рованное</a> спряжение, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переживать.html>пережива́ть</a> (2687)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пережить.html>пережи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perežítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переживать.html>пережива́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pereživátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пережить.html>пережи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to experience, to go through</li>
<li>to endure, to suffer, to ache</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be upset, to worry
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переживать.html>пережива́й</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>pereživáj</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">don't worry</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to survive, to outlive, to outlast, to self-survive
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пережить.html>переживу́</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja étovo ne <b>pereživú</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">This will kill me.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пережидать.html>пережида́ть</a> (21325)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-жида́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-židátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пережидать.html>пережида́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perežidátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переждать.html>пережда́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wait till (something) is over
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пережидать.html>пережида́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дождь.html>дождь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perežidátʹ</b> doždʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to wait till the rain is over [has stopped]</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***пережиток.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пережиток.html>пережи́ток</a> (18997)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пережить.html>пережи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perežítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ок</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пережиток.html>пережи́ток</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perežítok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пережиток.html>пережи́тка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пережиток.html>пережи́тки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пережиток.html>пережи́тков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>relic</li>
<li>survival</li>
<li>remnant, leftover, vestige
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пережиток.html>пережи́тки</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:феодализм.html>феодали́зма</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perežítki</b> feodalízma</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>feudal</b> vestiges</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>anachronism <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">person or thing which seems to belong to a different time</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>hangover, holdover</li>
<li>carryover</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перезарядить.html>перезаряди́вший</a> (28804)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перезарядить.html>перезаряди́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perezarjadívšij</span>)

<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перезарядить.html>перезаряди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perezarjadítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перезаряжать.html>перезаряжа́ть</a> (28078)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перезарядить.html>перезаряди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perezarjadítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***перезвонить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перезвонить.html>перезвони́ть</a> (17365)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звонить.html>звони́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zvonítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перезвонить.html>перезвони́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perezvonítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">перезва́нивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to ring again</li>
<li>to call back, to ring back, to call again <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">on the telephone</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:перезвонить.html>перезвоню́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вам</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смочь.html>смогу́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ja <b>perezvonjú</b> vam, kak tólʹko smogú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I will call/get back to you as soon as I can</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to ring (many or all bells)</li>
<li>to call (many or all people) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">on the telephone</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to ring louder than anything or anyone else</li></ol>

***переиграть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переиграть.html>переигра́ть</a> (19209)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:играть.html>игра́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">igrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переиграть.html>переигра́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pereigrátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переигрывать.html>переи́грывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to play again
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переиграть.html>переигра́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:игра.html>игру́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pereigrátʹ</b> igrú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to begin the game again; replay</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to overdo, to overact</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to beat, to get the better <i>(of)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to change, to shift around
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пока.html>пока́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переиграть.html>переигра́ли</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">poká tebjá ne býlo, my vsjó <b>pereigráli</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">while you were away, we changed all our plans</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:играть.html>игра́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">igrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыграть.html>сыгра́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sygrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переигрывать.html>переи́грывавший</a> (30105)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переигрывать.html>переи́грывавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pereígryvavšij</span>)
</p>

***переигрывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переигрывать.html>переи́грывать</a> (30105)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переиграть.html>переигра́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pereigrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переигрывать.html>переи́грывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pereígryvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переиграть.html>переигра́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to play again
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переигрывать.html>переи́грывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:игра.html>игру́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pereígryvatʹ</b> igrú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to begin the game again; replay</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to overdo, to overact
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переигрывать.html>переи́грывает</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>pereígryvajet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he overdoes it</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to beat, to get the better <i>(of)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to change, to shift around</li></ol>
